```html
<script>
window.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', () => {
  if (typeof window.modalOpenerHandler !== 'function') {
    window.modalOpenerHandler = function(e) {
      const opener = e.target.closest('[data-modal-opener]');
      if (!opener) return;

      e.preventDefault();
      e.stopPropagation();
      const id = opener.getAttribute('data-modal-opener');
      if (!id) return;

      const target = document.querySelector(`modal-opener[data-modal="#${id}"] button`);
      if (!target) return;
      target.click();
    };

    document.addEventListener('click', (e) => {
      const anchor = e.target.closest('a[data-modal-opener]');
      if (!anchor) return;
      e.preventDefault();
      e.stopPropagation();
      window.modalOpenerHandler(e);
    });
  }
});
</script>
```

```html
<script>
if (typeof initSliders === 'undefined') {
 const initSliders = (scope = document) => {
  scope.querySelectorAll('[data-collection-grid-slider]').forEach(slider => {
    const section = slider.closest('[data-id]');
    const container = slider.querySelector('.section-collection .slider__container');
    const slides = slider.querySelectorAll('[data-slide]');
    const btnPrev = slider.querySelector('.slider-button-prev');
    const btnNext = slider.querySelector('.slider-button-next');
    const currentEl = section.querySelector('.slider-counter--current');
    const totalEl = section.querySelector('.slider-counter--total');
    const progressFill = section.querySelector('.slider-progress-fill');

    const gap = 16;
    const totalSlides = slides.length;
    let currentIndex = 0;

    // Tính số lượng slide hiển thị trong khung
    const getVisibleSlides = () => {
      const containerWidth = container.clientWidth;
      const slideWidth = slides[0]?.offsetWidth || 1;
      return Math.floor((containerWidth) / (slideWidth));
    };

    const getSlideOffset = () => {
      if (slides.length < 2) return 0;
      return slides[1].offsetLeft - slides[0].offsetLeft;
    };

    const getTotalSteps = () => {
      const visibleSlides = getVisibleSlides();
      return Math.max(1, totalSlides - visibleSlides + 1);
    };

    const updateUI = () => {
      const slideOffset = getSlideOffset();
      const visibleSlides = getVisibleSlides();
      const totalSteps = getTotalSteps();
      if (totalSteps == 1) {
        if (slider.querySelector('.custom-slider-pagination ')) slider.querySelector('.custom-slider-pagination ').style.display = 'none';
        if (btnPrev) btnPrev.remove();
        if (btnNext) btnNext.remove();
        return 0;
      }
      const scrollLeft = container.scrollLeft;
      currentIndex = Math.round(scrollLeft / slideOffset);
      const currentStep = Math.min(currentIndex + 1, totalSteps);

      // Cập nhật số bước
      currentEl.textContent = String(currentStep).padStart(2, '0');
      totalEl.textContent = String(totalSteps).padStart(2, '0');

      // Thanh tiến trình
      const percent = totalSteps <= 1 ? 100 : ((currentStep - 1) / (totalSteps - 1)) * 100;
      progressFill.style.width = `${Math.min(percent, 100)}%`;

      // Nút điều hướng
      btnPrev.classList.toggle('disabled', currentIndex <= 0);
      btnNext.classList.toggle('disabled', currentIndex >= totalSteps - 1);
    };

    const scrollToIndex = (index) => {
      const slideOffset = getSlideOffset();
      const targetScroll = index * slideOffset;
      container.scrollTo({ left: targetScroll, behavior: 'smooth' });
      currentIndex = index;
      setTimeout(updateUI, 300);
    };

    btnNext?.addEventListener('click', () => {
      const totalSteps = getTotalSteps();
      if (currentIndex < totalSteps - 1) {
        scrollToIndex(currentIndex + 1);
      }
    });

    btnPrev?.addEventListener('click', () => {
      if (currentIndex > 0) {
        scrollToIndex(currentIndex - 1);
      }
    });

    container.addEventListener('scroll', () => {
      clearTimeout(container._scrollTimer);
      container._scrollTimer = setTimeout(updateUI, 100);
    });

    updateUI();
  });
};

document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', () => {
  initSliders();
});

let resizeTimer;
let lastIsWide = window.innerWidth > 750;
window.addEventListener('resize', () => {
  clearTimeout(resizeTimer);
  resizeTimer = setTimeout(() => {
    const isWide = window.innerWidth > 750;
    if (isWide !== lastIsWide) {
      initSliders();
      lastIsWide = isWide;
    }
  }, 200);
});

document.addEventListener('shopify:section:load', (event) => {
  const section = event.target;
  if (section.querySelector('[data-slider]')) {
    initSliders(section);
  }
  window.addEventListener('resize', () => {
    clearTimeout(resizeTimer);
    resizeTimer = setTimeout(() => {
      const isWide = window.innerWidth > 750;
      if (isWide !== lastIsWide) {
        initSliders();
        lastIsWide = isWide;
      }
    }, 200);
  });
});
} //end of define initSliders functions

</script>





</section>
```

- Tag: section
- Classes: shopify-section spaced-section spaced-section--full-width section--image-banner reveal-init reveal-visible show-image
- Headings: None

```html
<div id="Banner-template--20973157187736__image_banner_jkGfad" class="page-full banner-image-section">
```

```html
  <button aria-label="SHOP MIRA NECKLACE" data-target="" data-link="/products/mira-necklace" class="button base-button button--secondary use-base-color ">
    
    <span>SHOP MIRA NECKLACE</span>
    
      
    
  </button>
</base-button-component>

<script>
  (function () {
    class BaseButtonComponent extends HTMLElement {
      constructor() {
        super();
        this.addEventListener('click', this.onClickButton.bind(this));
      }

      onClickButton(e) {
        const button = e.target.closest('.base-button');
        if (button) {
          const link = button.getAttribute('data-link');
          const target = button.getAttribute('data-target');
          if (link) {
            e.preventDefault();
            if (Shopify && Shopify.designMode) {
              if (link.includes('https://') || link.includes('http://')) {
                if (window.confirm(`This link cannot be opened inside the editor. It will be opened in a new window (${link})`)) {
                  return;
                } else {
                  return;
                }
              }
            }
            if (target == '_blank') {
              window.open(link, '_blank').focus();
            } else {
              window.location.href = link;
            }
          }
        }
      }
    }

    if (!customElements.get('base-button-component')) {
      customElements.define('base-button-component', BaseButtonComponent);
    }
  })();
</script>

</div></div></div>
      </div>
    </div>
    </image-content-grid>
  </div>
</div>



</div>
```

```html
<script>
  // TAB FUNCTIONALITY
  function tabFunctionality() {
    const tabContainers = document.querySelectorAll('.tabs-container');

    tabContainers.forEach(container => {
      const tabLinks = container.querySelectorAll('.tabs-nav__link');
      const tabContents = container.querySelectorAll('.tab-content__item');

      function activateTab(targetId) {
        tabLinks.forEach(link => link.classList.remove('active'));
        tabContents.forEach(content => content.classList.remove('active'));

        const activeLink = container.querySelector(`[data-tab-target="${targetId}"]`);
        const activeContent = container.querySelector(`#${targetId}`);

        if (activeLink && activeContent) {
          activeLink.classList.add('active');
          activeContent.classList.add('active');
        }
      }

      tabLinks.forEach(link => {
        link.addEventListener('click', function (e) {
          e.preventDefault();
          const target = this.getAttribute('data-tab-target');
          activateTab(target);
          slideFunctionality();
        });
        link.addEventListener('keydown', function (e) {
          if (e.key === ' ' || e.key === 'Enter') {
            e.preventDefault();
            const target = this.getAttribute('data-tab-target');
            activateTab(target);
            slideFunctionality();
          }
        });
      });

      if (tabLinks.length > 0) {
        const defaultTarget = tabLinks[0].getAttribute('data-tab-target');
        activateTab(defaultTarget);
        slideFunctionality();
      }
    });
  }

  function slideFunctionality() {
      // SLIDER FUNCTIONALITY
    document.querySelectorAll('[data-collection-tabs-slider]').forEach(slider => {
      const scrollable = slider.querySelector('.slider_tabs');
      if (!scrollable) return;

      const slides = Array.from(slider.querySelectorAll('[data-slide]'));
      if (slides.length === 0) return;

      const btnPrev = slider.querySelector('.slider-button-prev');
      const btnNext = slider.querySelector('.slider-button-next');
      const currentEl = slider.querySelector('.slider-counter--current');
      const totalEl = slider.querySelector('.slider-counter--total');
      const progressFill = slider.querySelector('.slider-progress-fill');

      let currentIndex = 0;

      const getSlideOffset = () => {
        if (slides.length < 2) return 0;
        return slides[1].offsetLeft - slides[0].offsetLeft;
      };

       const getVisibleSlides = () => {
        const containerWidth = scrollable.clientWidth;
        const slideWidth = slides[0]?.offsetWidth || 1;
      
        let gap = 0;
        if (slides.length >= 2) {
          gap = slides[1].offsetLeft - slides[0].offsetLeft - slideWidth;
        }
      
        const fullSlideWidth = slideWidth + gap;
        if (fullSlideWidth <= 0) return 1; // tránh chia cho 0 hoặc âm
      
        return Math.floor((containerWidth + 0) / slideWidth);
      };

      const getTotalSteps = () => {
        const visibleSlides = getVisibleSlides();
        return Math.max(1, slides.length - visibleSlides + 1);
      };

      const scrollToIndex = (index) => {
        const slideOffset = getSlideOffset();
        const totalSteps = getTotalSteps();
        if (totalSteps == 1) {
          if (slider.querySelector('.custom-slider-pagination ')) slider.querySelector('.custom-slider-pagination ').style.display = 'none';
          if (btnPrev) btnPrev.remove();
          if (btnNext) btnNext.remove();
          return 0;
        }
        if (index < 0) index = 0;
        if (index >= totalSteps) index = totalSteps - 1;

        const targetScroll = slides[index]?.offsetLeft || 0;
        scrollable.scrollTo({
          left: targetScroll,
          behavior: 'smooth'
        });

        currentIndex = index;
        setTimeout(updateUI, 300);
      };

      const updateUI = () => {
        const totalSteps = getTotalSteps();
        if (totalSteps == 1) {
          if (slider.querySelector('.custom-slider-pagination ')) slider.querySelector('.custom-slider-pagination ').style.display = 'none';
          if (btnPrev) btnPrev.remove();
          if (btnNext) btnNext.remove();
          return 0;
        }
        const currentStep = Math.min(currentIndex + 1, totalSteps);

        if (currentEl) currentEl.textContent = String(currentStep).padStart(2, '0');
        if (totalEl) totalEl.textContent = String(totalSteps).padStart(2, '0');

        const percent = totalSteps <= 1 ? 100 : ((currentStep - 1) / (totalSteps - 1)) * 100;
        if (progressFill) progressFill.style.width = `${Math.min(percent, 100)}%`;

        btnPrev?.classList.toggle('disabled', currentIndex <= 0);
        btnNext?.classList.toggle('disabled', currentIndex >= totalSteps - 1);
      };

      btnNext?.addEventListener('click', () => {
        scrollToIndex(currentIndex + 1);
      });

      btnPrev?.addEventListener('click', () => {
        scrollToIndex(currentIndex - 1);
      });

      scrollable.addEventListener('scroll', () => {
        const slideOffset = getSlideOffset();
        const scrollLeft = scrollable.scrollLeft;
        const newIndex = Math.round(scrollLeft / slideOffset);
        if (newIndex !== currentIndex) {
          currentIndex = newIndex;
          updateUI();
        }
      });

      updateUI();
    });
  }

document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', () => {
  tabFunctionality();
  slideFunctionality();

  let resizeTimer;
  let lastIsWide = window.innerWidth > 750;
  window.addEventListener('resize', () => {
    clearTimeout(resizeTimer);
    resizeTimer = setTimeout(() => {
      const isWide = window.innerWidth > 750;
      if (isWide !== lastIsWide) {
        slideFunctionality();
        lastIsWide = isWide;
      }
    }, 200);
  });
});

  if (Shopify.designMode) {
    document.addEventListener("shopify:section:load", function (event) {
      tabFunctionality();
      slideFunctionality();
    });
    window.addEventListener('resize', () => {
      clearTimeout(resizeTimer);
      resizeTimer = setTimeout(() => {
        const isWide = window.innerWidth > 750;
        if (isWide !== lastIsWide) {
          tabFunctionality();
          slideFunctionality();
          lastIsWide = isWide;
        }
      }, 200);
    });
  }

</script>




</section>
```

## 13. shopify-section-template--20973157187736__shoppable_video_C8ak9y

- Tag: section
- Classes: shopify-section section section-shoppable-video reveal-init reveal-hidden
- Headings: Aurelia Pearl Necklace | Atria Pearl Necklace | Giulia Pearl Earrings | August Sardonyx Necklace

```html
<section id="shopify-section-template--20973157187736__shoppable_video_C8ak9y" class="shopify-section section section-shoppable-video reveal-init reveal-hidden"><link href="//poetic-theme-jewelry.myshopify.com/cdn/shop/t/59/assets/component-card.css?v=102937150194767392841773377586" rel="stylesheet" type="text/css" media="all">
<link href="//poetic-theme-jewelry.myshopify.com/cdn/shop/t/59/assets/component-price.css?v=75936967551694858061773377586" rel="stylesheet" type="text/css" media="all">
<link href="//poetic-theme-jewelry.myshopify.com/cdn/shop/t/59/assets/shop-video.css?v=2824105135719760801773377586" rel="stylesheet" type="text/css" media="all">
```
